 ) pakistan ke raashtrapati asif ali jaradaari ne shuukravaar komalala yusufjaike pita ko phone kar aatankwaadiyon ke krurtapurna hamale kii kadi ninda kii
 According to Geo News, Zardari expressed grief and sorrow for the Taliban attack on Malala during a telephone conversation with Zia-ud-din Yousafzai
 malala kii 'boli' ke aage taliban kii 'goli' felunhone kaha ki aatankwaadi is tarah kii ghatnaon ke jariye duniya ko apana asli cheharaa dikhaa rahe hai
 Zardari said that terrorists cannot move people and government resolutions by carrying out such incidents
 unhone kaha ki is ghatana ne logon kii aatankwaad ke khatre kaa saamana karne ke saahas ko nayaa bal diya he
 The President wished Malala to be well soon and said that the best wishes of the entire nation are with her
 bacchee se daraa taliban, saream maari goliunhone kaha ki malala khaybar pakhtoonkhwaa praant kii ladakiyon kii shiksha hasil karne kii ichha kii pratik he

 jaradaari ne kaha ki pakistan armd forces ke chikitsak ghayal malala kaa ilaaj kar rahe hai

 raashtrapati ne ghatana main ghayal hue malala ke doston ke prati bhi sahanubhuti jataayi

 balaatkaar ek aisa jurm he jisaki shikaar hui mahila ko hamaara samaaj hamaara tantra doshi se zyada doshi mahasoos kara detaa he
 There are laws, there are better laws than before, but those who enforce this law, what do the police think about a serious crime like rape
 
 
 
 Men, even male women police officers, hold the girl or the woman responsible for rape more than the rapist
 saare sawaal ladakiyon par hi uthe baat chaahe uske kapadon kii ho yaa vyavhaar kii yaa yahaan tak ki parivaar kii bhi
 Unfortunately, this situation belongs to the police of the capital and its adjoining areas
 isi biimaar soch ke maare 30 pulisavaalon kaa khulaasa kiya he tahalaka or enditivi ne
 Recently, a 28-year-old working girl was forcibly picked up by 6 men and gang-raped in a pub in Gurgaon
 kanoonee taur par to police balaatkaariyon kii talash kar rahi he lekin hakeekat main vah ladki kii nijee jindagi main galtiyaan talash rahi he
 Saying that the pub was not staffed but worked to bring customers there
 usee tarah dlef phej 2 ke esechao jansher singh balaatkaar ke aropiyon ko 'bachche' bataate hai or kehete hai ki umr kii badi ladki ne hi unhen bahakaaya
 Most policemen believe that rape is now a weapon of blackmailing
 17 se zyada afasaron kaa maananaa he ki yah sabakuch paise ke liye hota he
 Barely a month ago, the Noida police was horrified when it revealed the identity of a rape victim, a minor girl who was a victim of gang rape in a moving car
 is maamle main noida ke espi city ne peedit ladki par hi sawaal uthaae the lekin ab to had ho gai jab police vaale kah rahe hai ki agar koi ladki 10 ladakon ke saath car main baithti he to vah maasoom nahin ho sakati he? use pataa he ki ladakon ke saath sharaab pine kaa anjaam kya hoga? Policemen, who are ill-informed about rape, believe that 99 out of 100 cases of rape are false, only one to two per cent of cases are true
 ab ise pulisavaalon kaa ahsaan maane yaa phir unki beemaari ye faisla aap behatar kar sakate hai
 
 
 
 camere ke saamne yaa public ke saamne dilli police mahilaon kii suraksha ko lekar chaahe kitne bhi bade daawey kare lekin of da ricard unki soch kya he agar yah pataa chal jaae to logon kaa police se yakeen khatm ho jayega
 Think! a Delhi Police officer is openly saying that no rape takes place without the provocation of a girl child
 ladakiyon yaa mahilaon kii dress kya honi chahie ise lekar bahes hoti rahi he vakt-vakt par samaaj ke thekedaar ise lekar bayaan jari karte rahe hai
 Senior police officers have been commenting on women's dress
 un logon ne bayaan baad main bhale hi waapas le liya ho lekin ek aam pulisavaala jisase aam logon kaa vaasta padataa he vah puri mustaidi se yahi maanata he ki ladakiyon kii dress purushon ko rape ke liye uksaane kaa kaam karti he
 Regarding women from North East and other areas coming for livelihood in the capital and its adjoining areas, the police believe that they come here for earning but when the money is less, they accuse them of rape
 tippaniyan If the police are to be believed, then they do not accept their failure to be responsible for the incidents of rape
 Sometimes the responsibility of responsibility is blamed on the clothes and lifestyle of the girl and sometimes on the family and the home environment
 kya balaatkaar kii shikaayat karnaa kaarobaari soch kaa nateeja he
 
 
 
 kam se kam gudgaanv police to yahi maanati he jisaki pichley dinon khaasi chhichhaaledar bhi ho chuki he

 maine poocha ki dressing room main computer kya rahaa he
 He said, computer is not going to bat for me
 yah jahir khan yaa harbhajan singh ke liye gendbaaji bhi nahin karne vaala
 But over time i realized that the data kept in it can be seen within a few seconds
 agar main dekhnaa chahta hum ki 1999 yaa 2007 main maine australia main kisi ballebaaji kii, to yah paanch second main uplabdh he
 Tendulkar said, "if i want to see all straight drives, if i want to see all the balls left outside off side, it was available
" iske baad maine ise sweekaar kiya
 The veteran batsman said that the new technology helped him prepare better
 unhone kaha, iske baad chijen badal gayi
 This helped us to formulate a better strategy against the opponent, whatever be their weakness or strong side
 isse hamen madad mili
 It is just a question of experience and with time you accept all these things
 yah hamaare liye jivan kaa hissaa ban chukaa he
 The city of Latur, which was making headlines across the country due to last year's drought, is once again in the limelight
 vajah bana he yahaan kii mahanagar palika ke chunaav kaa nateeja
 Here the voters have raised the BJP from the floor and placed it on the harem
 latur main pani kii killat ne 2016 kii garmiyon main sabakaa dhyaan khinchaa
 Was the Chief Minister, Prime Minister and Railway Minister also seen worried about the water shortage of this city
 natijatan desh main sookhe se nibatane ke liye taatkaalik vikalp ke rup main pashchim maharashtra ke meraj se marathavada ke latur shahar ko rail wagon se pani supplai kar logon kii pyaas bujhaai gai
 It was called Latur Water Express
 is kavayad kii tab khub charchaa hui thi
 There was also a reason behind this that the former Chief Minister and veteran Congress leader Vilasrao Deshmukh used to go from this drought-prone area
 vilasarav kareeb saadhe aath saal maharashtra ke mukhyamantri rahe
 But there was no water from the tap in the area with a difference of one month
 bijepi ne maukey kii najaakat ko dekhte hue pani supplai kii muhim chalaai
 The comments sookhe main pani supplai ke badale main bijepi kii raajnneetik fasal ilaake main khub lahalhai
 Where the sun never set on the Congress power, after the water express was run in Latur, the Congress panicked in the Zilla Panchayat, Municipal Council and the results of Friday's counting were shocking
 bijepi ko us latur mahanagar palika main purna bahumat mila jahaan isse pehle vah sifer thi
 Chief Minister Devendra Fadnavis and Railway Minister Suresh Prabhu tweeted and thanked the voters
 jabaki rajya congress se latur mahanagar palika chunaav ke nateezon par koi pratikriya nahin ai he
 The water shortage in Latur caught everyone's attention in the summer of 2016
 kya mukhyamantri, pradhanmantri or railmantri tak is shahar kii pani kii killat ko lekar chintit dekhe gaye
 As a result, the thirst of the people was quenched by supplying water from a rail wagon to Miraj in western Maharashtra to Latur town of Marathwada as an immediate option to deal with the drought in the country
 ise latur water express kaha gaya
 There was a lot of discussion about this exercise then
 iske peeche yah bhi kaaran tha ki is suukhaagrast ilaake se rajya ke purv mukhyamantri or diggaj congressi netaa vilasarav deshmukh chunakar jate the
 Vilasrao was the Chief Minister of Maharashtra for nearly eight and a half years
 lekin ilaake main maheene bhar ke antar se nal se pani naseeb hota tha
 The BJP launched a water supply campaign in view of the opportunity
 tippaniyan In exchange for supplying water in the drought, the bjp's political crop stirred the area
 jahaan congress kii satta se suraj kabhi ast nahin hota tha us latur main water express chalane ke baad jila panchayat, nagar parishad main congress ne munh kii khai or shuukravaar kii matganana ke nattejey chaunkaane vaale rahe
 The BJP got an absolute majority in the Latur metropolitan municipality where it was earlier a cipher
